I know better.

I've brought my sketch book to do what I truly love.
Let's do this.
"""

DLG ITM_a
"""
-=-=-=-

-:DIARY ENTRY 3:-

The ocean is the giant soup of life.
As far as we know all life in the universe crawled from here.
"""

DLG ITM_b
"""
-=-=-=-

-:DIARY ENTRY 5:-

As I penetrate deeper into the ocean's belly the light dims.
Far off cloudy shapes take on ominous, terrible forms.
I dreamt of a gigantic dank chamber half filled with water.
The cement walls protruded straight from the black  liquid.
And as I looked down I became disoriented, lost.
Back up at me I saw gold-rimmed eyes emerge from deep down.
Fish eyes that do not focus, and soon the rest was visible.
But as my eyes focused on particulates and the fog...
...I could see that this was no ordinarily sized fish.
I could run minutes from end-to-end atop its dorsal fin.
But I wouldn't dare.

Soon I realized that many such giant fish were present.
Sooner I realized there was no ground beneath me.
As I fell into their water I knew awe and profound humility.
This is a feeling I have chased ever since.
This is a feeling I wish to capture and share.
"""

DLG ITM_c
"""
-=-=-=-

-:DIARY ENTRY 6:-

I'm not sure how much oxygen I have left in my tank.
I'm also unsure of how much more pressure this suit can take.
The creatures around me grow ever more ancient and strange.
The uncanny feeling of meeting a relative who lives far away.
We are all part of the tree of life, but we are so different.
These organisms have been around for so many eons...
...so much has happened while they haven't strayed far.
"""

DLG ITM_d
"""
-=-=-=-

-:DIARY ENTRY 7:-

It shouldn't be possible, but I reached the bottom.
I should be crushed like a grape under an elephant's foot.
Down here there is nothing but bottom-feeders with hard shells.
It's so dark now.
"""

DLG ITM_e
"""
-=-=-=-

-:DIARY ENTRY 8:-

My God. Can it be?

The captain's coordinates were right. Down here be treasure.
I have to take a closer look.
"""

DLG ITM_f
"""
It's beautiful.

There's enough here to make both the captain and me rich.
But, how can I carry this and my sketchbook at the same time?
Those sketches were the reason I took this job in the first place.
I can take enough treasure for the captain and the sketchbook...
...or I can leave the sketches behind.
"""

DLG ITM_g
"""
-=-=-=-

-:DIARY ENTRY 9:-

I told the captain that his map was wrong.
The treasure still remains hidden at the bottom of the sea.
I went back to the fishing village with my sketches.
What I had captured was something so few have seen.
Much like my dream... I needed to share it...
...so I took out a loan.
"""

DLG ITM_h
"""
It won't matter, though.

Nothing I do feels significant or meaningful anymore.
I look out my window and see my gardens and ramparts...
...I don't see the awe and humility that the ocean gave me.
It kills me.

That's why today I will be placing my fortune into a trust.
My charitable organizations will inherit all I own.
There are two items I am taking with me:
My boat.

And my diving suit.

I'll be going back for my real treasure.
"""

DLG ITM_i
"""
I rented a gallery for four months at the port.
All over tourists, fishermen, and bored locals came in.
Some didn't get it.

Some didn't see fish as terribly spectacular.
But...

Some people got it.

I'm not a wealthy man, and my diving days are over.
But finally I see that some people understand that feeling.
That feeling that the ocean invokes in us...
The feeling that it OUGHT to invoke.
And for that, I'm happy.
"""

DLG ITM_j
"""
-=-=-=-

-:DIARY ENTRY 9:-

The sea captain wasn't pleased to part with my share...
...but a deal is a deal.

First I bought simple things: fancy food and tailored suits.
Once I realized how much money I had things turned extravagant.
Fast cars, faster women, fastest drugs, and a castle.
I've since slowed down and do philanthropy work.
"""

DLG ITM_k
"""
-=-=-=-

-:DIARY ENTRY 4:-

There are creatures of all shapes and sizes here.

Anything that can work will thrive in the soup of life.
